```text
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">allPluginIds</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">forEach</span>((<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">id</span>) <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">></span> {
                <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">console</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">log</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">id</span>);
            })
        }
    };
}
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">export</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">default</span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">appTasks</span>,  <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> [<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">customPlugin</span>()]         <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
}
```
 
 

##### nodeDir

nodeDir: NormalizedFile
 
 
当前节点的根目录的NormalizedFile对象。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 

##### getNodeDir

getNodeDir: () => NormalizedFile

**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**返回值:**

| --- | --- |
| NormalizedFile | 当前节点的根目录的NormalizedFile对象 |
 
 
**示例：**

```text
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appTasks</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span>

    <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">return</span> {
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">pluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'customPlugin'</span>,
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">async</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">apply</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorNode</span>)<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">Promise</span><<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span>> {
           <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">dir</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getNodeDir</span>();
        }
    };
}
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">export</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">default</span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">appTasks</span>,  <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> [<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">customPlugin</span>()]         <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
}
```
 
 

##### addExtraOption

addExtraOption: (key: string, value: any) => void
 
为当前的node添加一个自定义属性。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| key | string | 是 | 要添加的自定义属性的key |
| value | any | 是 | 要添加的自定义属性的value |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 工程级hvigorfile.ts</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorNode</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorPlugin</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appTasks</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">export</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">function</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">customPlugin</span>()<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorPlugin</span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">return</span> {
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">pluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'customPlugin'</span>,
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">async</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">apply</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorNode</span>)<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">Promise</span><<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span>> {
           <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">addExtraOption</span>(<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'key'</span>, <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'value'</span>);
        }
    };
}
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">export</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">default</span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">appTasks</span>,  <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> [<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">customPlugin</span>()]         <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
}
```
 
 

##### getExtraOption

getExtraOption: (key: string) => any
 
获取通过addExtraOption()函数设置在当前node上的自定义属性。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| key | string | 是 | 自定义属性的key |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| any | 自定义属性的value |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
// 工程级hvigorfile.ts
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorNode</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorPlugin</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appTasks</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">export</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">function</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">customPlugin</span>()<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorPlugin</span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">return</span> {
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">pluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'customPlugin'</span>,
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">async</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">apply</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorNode</span>)<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">Promise</span><<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span>> {
           <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">addExtraOption</span>(<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'key'</span>, <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'value'</span>);
           <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getExtraOption</span>(<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'key'</span>);
        }
    };
}
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">export</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">default</span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">appTasks</span>,  <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> [<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">customPlugin</span>()]         <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
}
```
 
 

##### beforeNodeEvaluate

beforeNodeEvaluate(fn: (HvigorNode) => {}): void
 
为当前的node添加一个node评估前的回调函数。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| fn | (HvigorNode) => {} | 是 | 一个入参为空或者为HvigorNode的方法 |
 
 
**示例：**为名称为entry的node注册一个beforeNodeEvaluate hook并打印出node的信息。
 
```text
import { hvigor } from '@ohos/hvigor';
hvigor.nodesInitialized(() => {
  hvigor.getRootNode().subNodes(node => {
    if (node.getNodeName() === 'entry') {
      node.beforeNodeEvaluate(hvigorNode => {
        console.log(hvigorNode.getNodeName());
      })
    }
  })
});
```
 
 

##### afterNodeEvaluate

afterNodeEvaluate(fn: (HvigorNode) => {}): void
 
为当前的node添加一个node评估后的回调函数。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| fn | (HvigorNode) => {} | 是 | 一个入参为空或者为HvigorNode的方法 |
 
 
**示例：**为名称为entry的node注册一个afterNodeEvaluate hook并打印出node的信息。
 
```text
import { hvigor } from '@ohos/hvigor';
hvigor.nodesInitialized(() => {
  hvigor.getRootNode().subNodes(node => {
    if (node.getNodeName() === 'entry') {
      node.afterNodeEvaluate(hvigorNode => {
        console.log(hvigorNode.getNodeName());
      })
    }
  })
});
```
 
 

##### HvigorPlugin

该接口定义了Hvigor开发插件的基本范式。开发Hvigor插件需实现此接口。
 
 

##### 导入模块

```text
import { HvigorPlugin } from '@ohos/hvigor';
```
 
 

##### pluginId

pluginId: string
 
插件唯一标识属性。
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ HvigorNode, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorPlugin </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">实现自定义插件</span>
export function <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">customPlugin</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">HvigorPlugin </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    return <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">pluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'customPlugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
            return <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
                <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">data</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'customPlugin xxx'</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,</span>
        async <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">apply</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">HvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">Promise</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);"><</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">void</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">        }</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">    }</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);"> [</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">customPlugin</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>
```
 
 

##### context

context?: (() => any) | any
 
插件上下文实现接口，可选实现；实现此函数后，其他插件可通过node.getContext('插件ID'）获取插件中定义的上下文接口。
 

 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| (() => any) \| any | 自定义返回类型的Function或自定义任一返回类型 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorNode, HvigorPlugin </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">实现自定义插件</span>
export function <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">customPlugin</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">HvigorPlugin </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    return <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">pluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'customPlugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
            return <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
                <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">data</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'customPlugin xxx'</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,</span>
        async <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">apply</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">HvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">Promise</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);"><</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">void</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">        }</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">    }</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">[</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">customPlugin</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>
```
 
 

##### apply

apply: (node: HvigorNode) => void | Promise&lt;void&gt;
 
插件主体函数，用于定义插件实现逻辑（例如任务注册等）; 在Hvigor的生命周期配置阶段调用。
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| node | HvigorNode | 是 | hvigor节点对象 |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| void \| Promise&lt;void&gt; | 无返回值，或返回Promise&lt;void&gt;类型 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorPlugin </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">实现自定义插件</span>
export function <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">customPlugin</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">HvigorPlugin </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    return <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">pluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customPlugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
            return <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
                <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">data</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customPlugin xxx'</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
        async <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">apply</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">HvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">Promise</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);"><</span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">void</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span>async <span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
                <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">注册模块级任务</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">    }</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">customPlugin</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">()]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
```
 
 

##### HvigorTask

Hvigor任务实现的接口类型，定义了任务的实现范式，在创建任务时需实现此接口。
 
 

##### 导入模块

```text
import { HvigorTask } from '@ohos/hvigor';
```
 
 

##### name

name: string
 
定义任务名称。
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorTask </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">获取当前</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">节点对象</span>
const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">HvigorNode </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">注册</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">Task</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">registerTask</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">name</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customTask'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">run</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'this is Task'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
```
 
 

##### context

context?: (() => any) | any
 
任务中的局部内数据共享的对象定义。实现此函数中定义的对象将在任务注册时被注入到this.context属性上，在input、output、run函数中可使用直接this.context调用context函数中定义的对象和属性。
 

 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| (() => any) \| any | 自定义返回类型的Function或自定义任一返回类型 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorTask </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">获取当前</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">节点对象</span>
const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">HvigorNode </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">注册</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">Task</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">registerTask</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">name</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customTask'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        return <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">data</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customRegisterTask xxx'</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">run</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span>this<span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
```
 
 

##### input

input?: (input: TaskInput) => void
 
实现任务增量输入条件定义。
 

 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| input | TaskInput | 是 | 控制任务增量的输入条件实现对象 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorTaskContext</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">TaskInput</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">TaskOutput </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">"@ohos/hvigor"</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">fse </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">"fs-extra"</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">"path"</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getContext</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">) </span>as <span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">outputFilePath </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">resolve</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getBuildRootPath</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'test.txt'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">注册一个生成文件的任务并为此任务设置增量</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">registerTask</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">name</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">"testTask"</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">run</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">taskContext</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">HvigorTaskContext</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">void </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">| </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">Promise</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);"><</span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">void</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">fse</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">writeFileSync</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">outputFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getProjectName</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">())</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
            return undefined<span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">input</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">input</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">TaskInput</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">void </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">input</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">property</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'projectName'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getProjectName</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">())</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
        async <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">output</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">output</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">TaskOutput</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">Promise</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);"><</span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">void</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
            try <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
                const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">parentDir </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">dirname</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">outputFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
                await <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">fse</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">ensureDir</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">parentDir</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">; </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">确保父目录存在</span>
                await <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">fse</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">ensureFile</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">outputFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
                <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">output</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">file</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">outputFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>catch <span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">error</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">) </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
                <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">error</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'File creation failed:'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">error</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
                throw <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">error</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">        }</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">postDependencies</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'assembleApp'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">]</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor.     <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
```
 
需要在hvigor-config.json5中添加dependencies：
 
```json
// hvigor-config.json5
"dependencies": {
    "fs-extra": "11.2.0",
    "@types/fs-extra": "9.0.13"
},
```
 
 

##### output

output?: (output: TaskOutput) => void
 
实现任务增量输出条件定义。
 

 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| output | TaskOutput | 是 | 控制任务增量的输出条件实现对象 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text

import <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">fse </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">"fs-extra"</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">"path"</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">outputFilePath </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">resolve</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getBuildRootPath</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'test.txt'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">注册一个生成文件的任务并为此任务设置增量</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">registerTask</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>

        <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">run</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">taskContext</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">HvigorTaskContext</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">void </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">| </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">Promise</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);"><</span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">void</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">fse</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">writeFileSync</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">outputFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getProjectName</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">())</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
            return undefined<span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>

        async <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">output</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">output</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">TaskOutput</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">Promise</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);"><</span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">void</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
            try <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
                const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">parentDir </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">dirname</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">outputFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
                await <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">fse</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">ensureDir</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">parentDir</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">; </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">确保父目录存在</span>

            <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>catch <span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">error</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">) </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
                <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">error</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'File creation failed:'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">error</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor.     <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
```

 
 

##### run

run: (taskContext: HvigorTaskContext) => void | Promise&lt;void&gt;
 
任务执行逻辑主体函数。您可以在此函数实现中定义您所需的任务处理逻辑。
 

 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskContext | HvigorTaskContext | 否 | 接口中默认注入的公共信息类型 |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| void \| Promise&lt;void&gt; | 无返回值，或返回Promise&lt;void&gt;类型 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorTask </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">获取当前</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">节点对象</span>
const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">HvigorNode </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">注册</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">Task</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">registerTask</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">name</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customTask'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">run</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'this is Task'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
```
 
 

##### beforeRun

beforeRun?: (taskContext: HvigorTaskContext) => void | Promise&lt;void&gt;
 
run函数的前置处理函数。在任务执行阶段，任务中的run函数执行前此函数被调用执行。
 

 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskContext | HvigorTaskContext | 否 | 接口中默认注入的公共信息 |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| void \| Promise&lt;void&gt; | 无返回值，或返回Promise&lt;void&gt;类型 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">获取当前</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">节点对象</span>
const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">HvigorNode </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">注册</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">Task</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">registerTask</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">name</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customTask'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">run</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customTask'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">beforeRun</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'beforeRun'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
```
 
 

##### afterRun

afterRun?: (taskContext: HvigorTaskContext) => void | Promise&lt;void&gt;
 
run函数的后置处理函数。在任务执行阶段，任务中的run函数执行后此函数被调用执行。
 

 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskContext | HvigorTaskContext | 否 | 接口中默认注入的公共信息类型 |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| void \| Promise&lt;void&gt; | 无返回值，或返回Promise&lt;void&gt;类型 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorTask </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">获取当前</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">节点对象</span>
const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">HvigorNode </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">注册</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">Task</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">registerTask</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">name</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customTask'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">run</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customTask'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">afterRun</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'afterRun'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
```
 
 

##### dependencies

dependencies?: (() => string[]) | string[]
 
配置前置任务依赖。前置任务依赖是指当前任务依赖另一个任务，执行顺序是前置任务 -> 当前任务 -> 后置任务。
 
从DevEco Studio 6.0.0 Beta2版本开始，支持依赖其他模块的任务，在任务前加上“模块名:”即可，例如har:assembleHar。
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| (() => string[]) \| string[] | 返回类型为string[]的函数或string[]类型 |
 
 
> [!NOTE]
> 依赖其他模块的任务时，建议将任务注册操作放在 hook-nodesEvaluated 中，否则注册时其他模块的任务可能还未被初始化，导致当前任务无法注册。

 
**示例一：**依赖本模块的任务。
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorTask </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">获取当前</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">节点对象</span>
const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">HvigorNode </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">注册</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">Task</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">registerTask</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">name</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customTask'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">run</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customTask'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">dependencies</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customTask1'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">]</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">注册</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">Task</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">registerTask</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">name</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customTask1'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">run</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customTask1'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
```
 
 
**示例二：**依赖其他模块的任务。
 
```text
// 工程级hvigorfile.ts文件
import { appTasks } from '@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin';
import { hvigor, HvigorNode, HvigorPlugin } from '@ohos/hvigor';

// 获取当前entry节点对象
const entryNode = hvigor.getNodeByName('entry');

// 逻辑放在hook-nodesEvaluated中
hvigor.nodesEvaluated(async () => {
  // 注册任务
  entryNode.registerTask({
    // 任务名称
    name: `default@CustomTask`,
    run() {
      console.log('customTask1')
    },
    // 配置前置任务依赖
    dependencies: ['har:assembleHar'], // 跨模块依赖har的assembleHar任务，确保har模块存在
    // 配置任务的后置任务依赖
    postDependencies: ['entry:default@PreBuild']  // 支持两种写法 entry:default@PreBuild  default@PreBuild
  });
});

export default {
  system: appTasks, /* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */
  plugins: []       /* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */
}
```
 

##### postDependencies

postDependencies?: (() => string[]) | string[]
 
配置任务的后置任务依赖。后置任务依赖是指另一个任务依赖当前任务，执行顺序是前置任务 -> 当前任务 -> 后置任务。
 
从DevEco Studio 6.0.0 Beta2版本开始，支持依赖其他模块的任务，在任务前加上“模块名:”即可，例如har:default@PreBuild。
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| (() => string[]) \| string[] | 返回类型为string[]的函数或string[]类型 |
 
 
> [!NOTE]
> 依赖其他模块的任务时，建议将任务注册操作放在 hook-nodesEvaluated 中，否则注册时其他模块的任务可能还未被初始化，导致当前任务无法注册。

 
**示例一：**依赖本模块的任务。
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorTask </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">获取当前</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">节点对象</span>
const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">HvigorNode </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">注册</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">Task</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">registerTask</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">name</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'customTask1'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">run</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'customTask1'</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">注册</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">Task</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">registerTask</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">name</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customTask'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">run</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customTask'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">postDependencies</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'customTask1'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">]</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>


export default <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
```
 
 
**示例二：**依赖其他模块的任务。
 
```text
// 工程级hvigorfile.ts文件
import { appTasks } from '@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin';
import { hvigor, HvigorNode, HvigorPlugin } from '@ohos/hvigor';

// 获取当前entry节点对象
const entryNode = hvigor.getNodeByName('entry');

// 逻辑放在hook-nodesEvaluated中
hvigor.nodesEvaluated(async () => {
  // 注册任务
  entryNode.registerTask({
    // 任务名称
    name: `default@CustomTask`,
    run() {
      console.log('customTask1')
    },
    // 配置前置任务依赖
    dependencies: ['entry:default@PreBuild'], // 支持两种写法 entry:default@PreBuild  default@PreBuild
    // 配置任务的后置任务依赖
    postDependencies: ['har:default@PreBuild']  // 跨模块依赖har的PreBuild任务，确保har模块存在
  });
});

export default {
  system: appTasks, /* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */
  plugins: []       /* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */
}
```
 

##### HvigorTaskContext

Hvigor任务上下文对象类型，该类型的对象默认注册了当前任务的上下文信息。
 
 

##### 属性
 
| 成员 | 类型 | 只读 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| moduleName | string | 是 | 当前任务绑定的模块名称 |
| modulePath | string | 是 | 当前任务绑定的模块路径 |
 
 
 

##### TaskInput

任务增量执行判断的输入对象实现类型，提供添加任务输入条件的基本函数。
 
 

##### 导入模块

```text
import { TaskInput } from '@ohos/hvigor';
```
 
 

##### property

property(key: string, value: TaskInputValue): TaskInput
 
添加键值对作为Task增量输入条件。
 

 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| key | string | 是 | 条件名称 |
| value | TaskInputValue | 是 | 支持基本数组类型number、string、boolean及对应的数组类型的参数 |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| TaskInput | 当前控制任务增量的输入条件对象，用于链式调用 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorTask</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorTaskContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">TaskInput</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">TaskOutput </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">"@ohos/hvigor"</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">fse </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">"fs-extra"</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">"path"</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getContext</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">) </span>as <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">outputFilePath </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">resolve</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getBuildRootPath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'test.txt'</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">注册一个生成文件的任务并为此任务设置增量</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">registerTask</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">name</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">"testTask"</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,</span>
```
