```text
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">run</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">taskContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">HvigorTaskContext</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">void </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">| </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">Promise</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);"><</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">void</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">fse</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">writeFileSync</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">outputFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getProjectName</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">())</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
            return undefined<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">input</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">input</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">TaskInput</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">void </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">input</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">property</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'projectName'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getProjectName</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">())</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,</span>
        async <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">output</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">output</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">TaskOutput</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">Promise</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);"><</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">void</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
            try <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
                const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">parentDir </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">dirname</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">outputFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
                await <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">fse</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">ensureDir</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">parentDir</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">; </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">确保父目录存在</span>
                await <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">fse</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">ensureFile</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">outputFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
                <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">output</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">file</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">outputFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>catch <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">error</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">) </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
                <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">error</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'File creation failed:'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">error</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
                throw <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">error</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">        }</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">postDependencies</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">[</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'assembleApp'</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">]</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>
```
 
需要在hvigor-config.json5中添加dependencies：
 
```json
// hvigor-config.json5
"dependencies": {
    "fs-extra": "11.2.0",
    "@types/fs-extra": "9.0.13"
},
```
 
 

##### file

file(path: string): TaskInput
 
添加单个目录或文件路径作为任务增量输入条件。
 

 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| path | string | 是 | 目录或文件路径 |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| TaskInput | 当前控制任务增量的输入条件对象，用于链式调用 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 工程级hvigorfile.ts文件</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appTasks</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosAppContext</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getNode</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorTask</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorTaskContext</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">TaskInput</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">TaskOutput</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"@ohos/hvigor"</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"fs-extra"</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"path"</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getNode</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">__filename</span>);
<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">nodesEvaluated</span>(() <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">></span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getContext</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span>.<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span>) <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">as</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosAppContext</span>;
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">resolve</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getBuildRootPath</span>(), <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'testOutput.txt'</span>);
    <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 添加单个文件路径作为任务增量输入条件</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">inputFilePath</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">resolve</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getProjectPath</span>(), <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'testInput.txt'</span>); 
    <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 注册一个生成文件的任务并为此任务设置增量</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">registerTask</span>({
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">name</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"testTask"</span>,
        <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">run</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">taskContext</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorTaskContext</span>)<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">|</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">Promise</span><<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span>> {
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">parentDir</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">dirname</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span>);
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">ensureDirSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">parentDir</span>); <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 确保父目录存在</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">ensureFileSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span>);
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">writeFileSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getProjectName</span>());
            <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">return</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">undefined</span>;
        },
        <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">input</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">input</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">TaskInput</span>)<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span> {
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">input</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">property</span>(<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'projectName'</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getProjectName</span>());
            <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">if</span> (<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">existsSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">inputFilePath</span>)) {
                <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">input</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">file</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">inputFilePath</span>);
            }
        },
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">async</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">output</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">output</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">TaskOutput</span>)<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">Promise</span><<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span>> {
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">output</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">file</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span>);
        },
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">postDependencies</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> [<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'assembleApp'</span>]
    })
})
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">export</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">default</span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">appTasks</span>,  <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span>[]         <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
}
```
 
 
需要在hvigor-config.json5中添加dependencies：
 
```json
// hvigor-config.json5
"dependencies": {
    "fs-extra": "11.2.0",
    "@types/fs-extra": "9.0.13"
},
```
 

##### files

files(paths: string[]): TaskInput
 
添加多个目录或文件路径作为任务增量输入条件。
 

 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| paths | string | 是 | 目录或文件路径列表 |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| TaskInput | 当前控制任务增量的输入条件对象，用于链式调用 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 工程级hvigorfile.ts文件</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appTasks</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosAppContext</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getNode</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorTask</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorTaskContext</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">TaskInput</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">TaskOutput</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"@ohos/hvigor"</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"fs-extra"</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"path"</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getNode</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">__filename</span>);
<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">nodesEvaluated</span>(() <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">></span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getContext</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span>.<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span>) <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">as</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosAppContext</span>;
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">resolve</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getBuildRootPath</span>(), <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'test.txt'</span>);
    <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 添加单个文件路径作为任务增量输入条件。</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">inputFilePath</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">resolve</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getProjectPath</span>(), <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'test.txt'</span>); 
    <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 注册一个生成文件的任务并为此任务设置增量</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">registerTask</span>({
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">name</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"testTask"</span>,
        <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">run</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">taskContext</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorTaskContext</span>)<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">|</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">Promise</span><<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span>> {
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">parentDir</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">dirname</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span>);
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">ensureDirSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">parentDir</span>); <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 确保父目录存在</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">ensureFileSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span>);
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">writeFileSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getProjectName</span>());
            <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">return</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">undefined</span>;
        },
        <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">input</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">input</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">TaskInput</span>)<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span> {
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">input</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">property</span>(<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'projectName'</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getProjectName</span>());
            <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">if</span> (<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">existsSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">inputFilePath</span>)) {
                <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">input</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">files</span>([<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">inputFilePath</span>, ]);
            }
        },
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">async</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">output</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">output</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">TaskOutput</span>)<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">Promise</span><<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span>> {
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">output</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">files</span>([<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span>,]);
        },
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">postDependencies</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> [<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'assembleApp'</span>]
    })
})
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">export</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">default</span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">appTasks</span>,  <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span>[]         <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
}
```
 
 
需要在hvigor-config.json5中添加dependencies：
 
```json
// hvigor-config.json5
"dependencies": {
    "fs-extra": "11.2.0",
    "@types/fs-extra": "9.0.13"
},
```
 

##### TaskOutput

任务增量执行判断的输出对象实现类型，提供添加任务输出条件的基本函数。
 
 

##### 导入模块

```text
import { TaskOutput } from '@ohos/hvigor';
```
 
 

##### file

file(path: string): TaskOutput
 
添加单个目录或文件路径作为任务的增量输出条件。
 

 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| path | string | 是 | 目录或文件路径 |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| TaskOutput | 当前控制任务增量的输出条件对象，用于支持链式调用 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 工程级hvigorfile.ts文件</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appTasks</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosAppContext</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getNode</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorTaskContext</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">TaskInput</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">TaskOutput</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"@ohos/hvigor"</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"fs-extra"</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"path"</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getNode</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">__filename</span>);
<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">nodesEvaluated</span>(() <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">></span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getContext</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span>.<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span>) <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">as</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosAppContext</span>;
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">resolve</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getBuildRootPath</span>(), <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'testOutput.txt'</span>);
    <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 添加单个文件路径作为任务增量输入条件</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">inputFilePath</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">resolve</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getProjectPath</span>(), <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'testInput.txt'</span>); 
    <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 注册一个生成文件的任务并为此任务设置增量</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">registerTask</span>({
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">name</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"testTask"</span>,
        <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">run</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">taskContext</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorTaskContext</span>)<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">|</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">Promise</span><<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span>> {
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">parentDir</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">dirname</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span>);
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">ensureDirSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">parentDir</span>); <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 确保父目录存在</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">ensureFileSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span>);
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">writeFileSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getProjectName</span>());
            <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">return</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">undefined</span>;
        },
        <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">input</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">input</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">TaskInput</span>)<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span> {
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">input</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">property</span>(<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'projectName'</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getProjectName</span>());
            <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">if</span> (<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">existsSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">inputFilePath</span>)) {
                <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">input</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">file</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">inputFilePath</span>);
            }
        },
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">async</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">output</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">output</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">TaskOutput</span>)<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">Promise</span><<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span>> {
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">output</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">file</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span>);
        },
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">postDependencies</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> [<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'assembleApp'</span>]
    })
})
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">export</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">default</span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">appTasks</span>,  <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span>[]         <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
}
```
 
需要在hvigor-config.json5中添加dependencies：
 
```json
// hvigor-config.json5
"dependencies": {
    "fs-extra": "11.2.0",
    "@types/fs-extra": "9.0.13"
},
```
 
 

##### files

files(paths: string[]): TaskOutput
 
添加多个目录或文件路径作为任务的增量输出条件。
 

 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| paths | string[] | 是 | 目录或文件路径列表 |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| TaskOutput | 控制任务增量的输出条件对象，用于支持链式调用 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 工程级hvigorfile.ts文件</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appTasks</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosAppContext</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getNode</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorTaskContext</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">TaskInput</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">TaskOutput</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"@ohos/hvigor"</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"fs-extra"</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"path"</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getNode</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">__filename</span>);
<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">nodesEvaluated</span>(() <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">></span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getContext</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span>.<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span>) <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">as</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosAppContext</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">    const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">resolve</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getBuildRootPath</span>(), <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'testOutput.txt'</span>);
    <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 添加单个文件路径作为任务增量输入条件。</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">inputFilePath</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">resolve</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getProjectPath</span>(), <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'testInput.txt'</span>); 
    <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 注册一个生成文件的任务并为此任务设置增量</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">registerTask</span>({
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">name</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"testTask"</span>,
        <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">run</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">taskContext</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorTaskContext</span>)<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">|</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">Promise</span><<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span>> {
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">parentDir</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">dirname</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span>);
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">ensureDirSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">parentDir</span>); <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">// 确保父目录存在</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">ensureFileSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span>);
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">writeFileSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getProjectName</span>());
            <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">return</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">undefined</span>;
        },
        <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">input</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">input</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">TaskInput</span>)<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span> {
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">input</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">property</span>(<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'projectName'</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getProjectName</span>());
            <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">if</span> (<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">fse</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">existsSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">inputFilePath</span>)) {
                <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">input</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">files</span>([<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">inputFilePath</span>, ]);
            }
        },
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">async</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">output</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">output</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">TaskOutput</span>)<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">Promise</span><<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span>> {
            <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">output</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">files</span>([<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">outputFilePath</span>,]);
        },
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">postDependencies</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> [<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'assembleApp'</span>]
    })
})
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">export</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">default</span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">appTasks</span>,  <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span>[]         <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
}
```
 
 
需要在hvigor-config.json5中添加dependencies：
 
```json
// hvigor-config.json5
"dependencies": {
    "fs-extra": "11.2.0",
    "@types/fs-extra": "9.0.13"
},
```
 

##### Task

HvigorTask的外置对象。您可以使用此对象访问任务的属性、 操作任务提供的接口函数。
 
 

##### 导入模块

```text
import { Task } from '@ohos/hvigor';
```
 
 

##### getName

getName: () => string
 
 
获取任务名称。
 

 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| string | 任务名称 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">Task </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">rootNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getRootNode</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">assembleAppTask</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">Task </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">| </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">undefined </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">rootNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getTaskByName</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'assembleApp'</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    if <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">assembleAppTask</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">) </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
        const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">taskName </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">assembleAppTask</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getName</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`taskName: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">${</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">taskName</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>
```
 

##### getDependencies

getDependencies: () => string[]
 
 
获取当前任务依赖的前置任务名称列表。
 

 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| string[] | 当前任务依赖的前置任务名称列表 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);"> } </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">Task </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">rootNode </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getRootNode</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">assembleAppTask</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">Task </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">| </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">undefined </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">rootNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getTaskByName</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'assembleApp'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    if <span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">assembleAppTask</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">) </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">taskDependencies </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">assembleAppTask</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getDependencies</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">`Task Dependencies: </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">${</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">taskDependencies</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">`</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
```
 

##### setEnable

setEnable: (enable: boolean) => void
 
设置任务的启用状态，当任务被禁用时，任务仍然在任务依赖图中存在，仅跳过了任务的执行，不会破坏原来设定的任务依赖关系。任务被注册时任务状态默认是启用的。
 

 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| enable | boolean | 是 | true：启用任务， false: 禁用任务 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosHapContext</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId, Target </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">HvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);"> } </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">rootNode </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getRootNode</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">rootNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">subNodes</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">((</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">HvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">) </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">获取</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hap</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">模块上下文信息</span>
        const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hapContext </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getContext</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OHOS_HAP_PLUGIN</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">) </span>as <span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">OhosHapContext</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
        const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">moduleName </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hapContext</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">?.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getModuleName</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hapContext</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">?.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">targets</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">((</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">target</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">Target</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">) </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">禁用任务</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getTaskByName</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">`</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">${</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">target</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getTargetName</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">@SignHap`</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">?.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">setEnable</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span>false<span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
```
 
 

##### beforeRun

beforeRun: (fn: Function) => void
 
添加任务执行之前的钩子函数。钩子函数以栈结构存储，遵循先进后出原则，后添加的函数先被执行。
 

 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| fn | Function | 是 | 回调函数 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);"> } </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">Task </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">rootNode </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getRootNode</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">assembleAppTask</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">Task </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">| </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">undefined </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">rootNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getTaskByName</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'assembleApp'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    if <span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">assembleAppTask</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">) </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">任务执行之前的钩子函数</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">assembleAppTask</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">beforeRun</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'Before Task: assembleApp'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
```
 
 

##### afterRun

afterRun: (fn: Function) => void
 
 
添加任务执行完成之后的钩子函数。钩子函数以堆结构存储，遵循先进先出原则，先添加的函数先被执行。
 

 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| fn | Function | 是 | 回调函数 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);"> } </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">Task </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">rootNode </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getRootNode</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">assembleAppTask</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">Task </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">| </span><span style="color: rgb(204,120,50);">undefined </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">rootNode</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">getTaskByName</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'assembleApp'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    if <span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">assembleAppTask</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">) </span><span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">任务执行之后的钩子函数</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">assembleAppTask</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">afterRun</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
            <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(101,204,225);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(170,125,252);">'After Task: assembleApp'</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">;</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(226,218,144);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(219,126,155);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(250,162,61);">}</span>
```
 

##### SdkDetails

应用工程使用的SDK相关的信息。在调用SdkDetails的接口前，可以先通过OhosAppContext的[getSdkDetails](https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/ide-build-expanding-context#section085712212299)方法来获取本对象。
 
 

##### 导入模块

```text
import { SdkDetails } from '@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin';
```
 
 

##### getSdkDir

getSdkDir: () => string
 
获取SDK所在目录。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 6.0.4
 
**返回值：**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| string | SDK所在目录 |
 
 
在工程级hvigorfile.ts中编写示例代码：
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appTasks, OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">SdkDetails </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor, HvigorNode, HvigorPlugin </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

export function <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">customPlugin</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorPlugin </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
  return <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">pluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">'customPlugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
      return <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">data</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">'customPlugin xxx'</span>
      <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,</span>
    async <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">apply</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">Promise</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);"><</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
      <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">afterNodeEvaluate</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">node </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
        const <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appContext </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getContext</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">) </span>as <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
        if <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appContext</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">) </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
          let <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">sdk</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">SdkDetails </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getSdkDetails</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
          <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">sdk</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">?.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getSdkDir</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">())</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">      }</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">  }</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">}</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
  <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
  <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">[</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">customPlugin</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">()]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">}</span>
```
 
 

##### isOhos

isOhos: () => boolean
 
判断是否为OpenHarmony SDK。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 6.0.4
 
**返回值：**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| boolean | 是否为OpenHarmony SDK |
 
 
在工程级hvigorfile.ts中编写示例代码：
 
```text

      return <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>

      <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,</span>
    async <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">apply</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">Promise</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);"><</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
      <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">afterNodeEvaluate</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">node </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
        const <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appContext </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getContext</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">) </span>as <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
        if <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appContext</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">) </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
          let <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">sdk</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">SdkDetails </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getSdkDetails</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

        <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">}</span>

    <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">  }</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
```

##### getSdkVersion

getSdkVersion: () => number

##### getEtsComponentVersion

##### getEtsComponentReleaseType

getEtsComponentReleaseType: () => string
 
获取SDK中ets组件（DevEco Studio安装目录/sdk/default/openharmony/ets目录下的组件）的发布类型值。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 6.0.4
 
**返回值：**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| string | 获取SDK中ets组件发布类型值 |
 
 
在工程级hvigorfile.ts中编写示例代码：
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appTasks </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);"> OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);"> SdkDetails </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor, HvigorNode, HvigorPlugin </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

export function <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">customPlugin</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorPlugin </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
  return <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">pluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">'customPlugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
      return <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">data</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">'customPlugin xxx'</span>
      <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,</span>
    async <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">apply</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">HvigorNode</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">Promise</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);"><</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">void</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
      <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">afterNodeEvaluate</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">node </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
        const <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appContext </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getContext</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">) </span>as <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
        if <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appContext</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">) </span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">{</span>
          let <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">sdk</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">SdkDetails </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getSdkDetails</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
```
