```text
  <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">[</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">customPlugin</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">()]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">}</span>
```
 
 

##### NormalizedFile

hvigor API中的文件类。您可以通过此对象来进行一些基本的文件操作。
 
 

##### filePath

filePath: string
 
当前对象的路径信息。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);"> } </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">rootNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getRootNode</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">moduleNormalizedFile </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">rootNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">nodeDir</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`Module Normalized File Path: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">${</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">moduleNormalizedFile</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">filePath</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>
```

| --- | --- |

**示例：**
 
```text

    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">rootNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getRootNode</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`Module Normalized File Path: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">${</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">moduleNormalizedFile</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getPath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
```

##### file

file: (_path: string) => NormalizedFile
 
在原有的目录路径链式拼接路径，获取它的NormalizedFile对象。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| _path | string | 是 | 需要拼接路径字符串 |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| NormalizedFile | 在原有的NormalizedFile对象的路径链式拼接所得到NormalizedFile对象 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```json
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);"> } </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">rootNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getRootNode</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">moduleNormalizedFile </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">rootNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">nodeDir</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">buildProfileNormalizedFile </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">moduleNormalizedFile</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">file</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'build-profile.json5'</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`buildProfile File Path: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">${</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">buildProfileNormalizedFile</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getPath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>
```
 
 

##### asFileList

asFileList: () => NormalizedFile[]
 
获取到NormalizedFile对象下深层递归的目录与文件NormalizedFile[]，包含它本身。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| NormalizedFile[] | NormalizedFile对象下深层递归的目录与文件NormalizedFile[]，包含它本身 |
 
 
当前只能通过node节点的 node.nodeDir 或者 node.node.getNodeDir() 获取该node节点的根路径的NormalizedFile对象，再通过NormalizedFile.file(_path: string)方法拼接后续路径来获取到新的NormalizedFile对象，工程级hvigorfile.ts示例：
 
```json
<span style="color: rgb(207,142,109);">import </span>{ <span style="color: rgb(86,168,245);">appTasks </span>} <span style="color: rgb(207,142,109);">from </span><span style="color: rgb(106,171,115);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">导入接口</span>
<span style="color: rgb(207,142,109);">import </span>{ HvigorPlugin, HvigorNode} <span style="color: rgb(207,142,109);">from </span><span style="color: rgb(106,171,115);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">实现自定义插件</span>
<span style="color: rgb(207,142,109);">function </span><span style="color: rgb(86,168,245);">customPlugin</span>(): HvigorPlugin {
    <span style="color: rgb(207,142,109);">return </span>{
        <span style="color: rgb(199,125,187);">pluginId</span>: <span style="color: rgb(106,171,115);">'customPlugin'</span>,
        <span style="color: rgb(86,168,245);">apply</span>(node: HvigorNode) {
            <span style="color: rgb(86,168,245);">appTask</span>(node);
        }
    }
}
<span style="color: rgb(207,142,109);">function </span><span style="color: rgb(86,168,245);">appTask</span>(currentNode: HvigorNode) {
    <span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">工程级的</span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">node</span>
    currentNode.<span style="color: rgb(86,168,245);">subNodes</span>((node: HvigorNode) => {
        <span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">模块级的</span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">node </span>
<span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">        // </span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">通过</span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">node.nodeDir </span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">或者</span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);"> node.node.getNodeDir() </span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">获取该</span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">node</span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">节点的根路径的</span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">NormalizedFile</span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">文件</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(207,142,109);">const </span><span style="color: rgb(169,183,198);">moduleNormalizedFile </span>= node.<span style="color: rgb(199,125,187);">nodeDir</span>;
        <span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">通过</span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">NormalizedFile.file() </span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">拼接后续路径，生成新的</span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);"> NormalizedFile </span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">对象</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">生成模块下面</span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);"> build-Profile.json5 </span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">的</span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);"> NormalizedFile </span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">对象</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(207,142,109);">const </span><span style="color: rgb(111,115,122);">buildProfileNormalizedFile </span>= <span style="color: rgb(169,183,198);">moduleNormalizedFile</span>.<span style="color: rgb(86,168,245);">file</span>(<span style="color: rgb(106,171,115);">'build-profile.json5'</span>);
    })
}
<span style="color: rgb(207,142,109);">export default </span>{
    <span style="color: rgb(199,125,187);">system</span>: <span style="color: rgb(86,168,245);">appTasks</span>,  <span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(199,125,187);">plugins</span>:[
        <span style="color: rgb(86,168,245);">customPlugin</span>()  <span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">应用自定义</span><span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">Plugin</span>
    ]         <span style="color: rgb(122,126,133);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
}
```
 
 

##### FileUtil

文件操作工具类，支持一些基本的文件操作。
 
 

##### 导入模块

```text
import { FileUtil } from '@ohos/hvigor';
```
 
 

##### exist

exist: (filePath: string) => boolean
 
判断文件路径是否存在。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| filePath | string | 是 | 文件路径字符串 |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| boolean | true: 文件路径存在，false: 文件路径不存在 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appTasks</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosAppContext</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">FileUtil</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getNode</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"path"</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getNode</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">__filename</span>);
<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">nodesEvaluated</span>(() <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">></span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getContext</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span>.<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span>) <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">as</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosAppContext</span>;
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">testFilePath</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">resolve</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getProjectPath</span>(), <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'test.txt'</span>);
    <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">if</span> (<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">FileUtil</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">exist</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">testFilePath</span>)) {
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">console</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">log</span>(<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">`File exists: </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">${</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">testFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">`</span>);
    } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">else</span> {
        <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">console</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">log</span>(<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">`File doesn't exist: </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">${</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">testFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">`</span>);
    }
})
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">export</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">default</span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">appTasks</span>,  <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span>[]         <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
}
```
 
 

##### isDictionary

isDictionary: (file: string | NormalizedFile) => boolean
 
判断文件路径或NormalizedFile对象是否是目录。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| file | string \| NormalizedFile | 是 | 文件路径字符串或者是NormalizedFile对象 |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| boolean | true: 是目录，false: 不是目录 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosAppContext </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">"path"</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getContext</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">) </span>as <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">testFilePath </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">resolve</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getProjectPath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'test.txt'</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">ensureFileSync</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">testFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    if <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">isDictionary</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">testFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)) </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`It is a directory: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">${</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">testFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>else <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`It is not a directory: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">${</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">testFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>
```
 
 

##### isFile

isFile: (file: string | NormalizedFile) => boolean
 
判断文件路径或NormalizedFile对象是否是文件。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| file | string \| NormalizedFile | 是 | 文件路径字符串或者是NormalizedFile对象 |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| boolean | true: 是文件，false: 不是文件 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosAppContext </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">"path"</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getContext</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">) </span>as <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">testFilePath </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">resolve</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getProjectPath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'test.txt'</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">ensureFileSync</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">testFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    if <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">isFile</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">testFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)) </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`It is a file: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">${</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">testFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>else <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
        <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`It is not a file: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">${</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">testFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>
```
 
 

##### ensureDirSync

ensureDirSync: (dirPath: string) => void
 
确保目录存在，不存在就创建。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| dirPath | string | 是 | 目标目录地址 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">appTasks</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosAppContext</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> { <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">FileUtil</span>, <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getNode</span> } <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">import</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">from</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">"path"</span>;
<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getNode</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">__filename</span>);
<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">hvigor</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">nodesEvaluated</span>(() <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">></span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">const</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span> <span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">=</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">currentNode</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getContext</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosPluginId</span>.<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span>) <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">as</span> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">OhosAppContext</span>;   
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">FileUtil</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">ensureDirSync</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">path</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">dirname</span>(<span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">context</span>.<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">getBuildRootPath</span>()));
})
<span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">export</span> <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">default</span> {
    <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">appTasks</span>,  <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">:</span>[]         <span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
}
```
 
 

##### ensureFileSync

ensureFileSync: (filePath: string) => void
 
确保文件存在，不存在就创建。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| filePath | string | 是 | 目标文件地址 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```text
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosAppContext </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">"path"</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getContext</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">) </span>as <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">testFilePath </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">resolve</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getProjectPath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'test.txt'</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">ensureFileSync</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">testFilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>
```

##### readJson5

readJson5: (file: string | NormalizedFile) => JSON
 
同步读取Json5文件。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| file | string \| NormalizedFile | 是 | json5文件路径或者NormalizedFile对象 |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| JSON | 读取出的JSON格式数据 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```json
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosAppContext </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">"path"</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getContext</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">) </span>as <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">resolve</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getProjectPath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'testJson.json5'</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">ensureFileSync</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">writeFileSync</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">JSON</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">stringify</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getAppJsonOpt</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()))</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">jsonContent </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">readJson5</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`Read JSON5 content: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">${</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">JSON</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">stringify</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">jsonContent</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span>null<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">2</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>
```

##### readFileSync

readFileSync: (file: string | NormalizedFile) => Buffer
 
同步读取文件。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| Buffer | 读取的Buffer数据 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```json

import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosAppContext </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">"path"</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getContext</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">) </span>as <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">resolve</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getProjectPath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'testJson.json5'</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">ensureFileSync</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span>


export default <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. ##### readFile
```

readFile: (file: string | NormalizedFile) => Promise&lt;Buffer&gt;
 
异步读取文件。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| file | string \| NormalizedFile | 是 | 文件路径字符串或者是NormalizedFile对象 |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| Promise | Promise&lt;Buffer&gt; |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```json
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>

import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">"path"</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span>async <span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">() </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getContext</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">) </span>as <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">resolve</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getProjectPath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'testJson.json5'</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">ensureFileSync</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">writeFileSync</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">JSON</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">stringify</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getAppJsonOpt</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()))</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">content </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span>await <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">readFile</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">content</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">toString</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">())</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span>


export default <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor.     <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>

```
 
 

##### writeFileSync

writeFileSync: (file: string | NormalizedFile, content: any) => void
 
同步写入文件。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| file | string \| NormalizedFile | 是 | 文件路径字符串或者是NormalizedFile对象 |
| content | any | 是 | 需要写入文件的内容 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```json
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosAppContext </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">"path"</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getContext</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">) </span>as <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">resolve</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getProjectPath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'testJson.json5'</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">ensureFileSync</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">writeFileSync</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">JSON</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">stringify</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getAppJsonOpt</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()))</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">jsonContent </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">readJson5</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">console</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">log</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`Read JSON5 content: </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">${</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">JSON</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">stringify</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">jsonContent</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span>null<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(80,160,79);">2</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">`</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor.     <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>
```

##### writeFile

writeFile: (file: string | NormalizedFile, content: any) => Promise&lt;void&gt;
 
异步写入文件。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| file | string \| NormalizedFile | 是 | 文件路径字符串或者是NormalizedFile对象 |
| content | any | 是 | 需要写入文件的内容 |
 
 
**返回值:**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| Promise | Promise&lt;void&gt; |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```json
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosAppContext </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">"path"</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getContext</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">) </span>as <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">path</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">resolve</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getProjectPath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'testJson.json5'</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">ensureFileSync</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">writeFile</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">json5FilePath</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">JSON</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">stringify</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getAppJsonOpt</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">()))</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span>

export default <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">system</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">: </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">,  </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */</span>
    <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">plugins</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">:</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">[]         </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">/* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */</span>
<span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">}</span>
```

##### copyFileSync

copyFileSync: (file: string | NormalizedFile, dest: string) => void
 
同步复制文件。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 4.3.0
 
**参数:**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| file | string \| NormalizedFile | 是 | 文件路径字符串或者是NormalizedFile对象 |
| dest | string | 是 | 目标文件路径 |
 
 
**示例：**
 
```json
<span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">// </span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">工程级</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">hvigorfile.ts</span><span style="color: rgb(128,128,128);">文件</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">appTasks</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosAppContext </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
import <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{ </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">FileUtil</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">, </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">getNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">} </span>from <span style="color: rgb(132,63,161);">'@ohos/hvigor'</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getNode</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">__filename</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">)</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>

<span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">hvigor</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">nodesEvaluated</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(() </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">=</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">></span> <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">{</span>
    const <span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">context </span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">= </span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">currentNode</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,255);">getContext</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">(</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OhosPluginId</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">.</span><span style="color: rgb(255,255,255);">OHOS_APP_PLUGIN</span><span style="color: rgb(255,0,170);">) </span>as <span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">OhosAppContext</span><span style="color: rgb(181,106,1);">;</span>
```

| dest | string | 是 | 目标文件路径 |

##### submitWorker

submitWorker(node: HvigorNode, taskName: string, workPath: string, workerOption: WorkerOption): TCB
 
向线程池提交一个worker并执行，worker必须归属于某个任务，表示这个任务并没有结束，但此时主线程可以执行其他任务，依赖该任务的其他任务仍然会排队等待。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 6.0.4
 
**参数：**
  
| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| node | HvigorNode | 是 | worker归属的任务对应的节点。 |
| taskName | string | 是 | 向线程池提交worker的任务名称。 |
| workPath | string | 是 | 要执行的worker的文件路径，可以拼接函数名称，例如D:/xx/a.js/run是指运行a.js的run方法。 |
| workerOption | WorkerOption | 是 | worker配置。 |
 
 
**返回值：**
  
| 类型 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| TCB | 提交的worker的状态。 |
 
 
**示例：**在hap模块的自定义任务中，向线程池提交一个worker。
 
```text
import { hapTasks } from '@ohos/hvigor-ohos-plugin';
import { HvigorNode, HvigorPlugin, submitWorker } from "@ohos/hvigor";
import path from "path";

// 实现自定义插件
function customPlugin(): HvigorPlugin {
  return {
    pluginId: 'customPlugin',
    apply(node: HvigorNode) {
      // 插件主体
      node.registerTask({
        name: 'customTask',
        run() {
          submitWorker(node, this.name, path.join(__dirname, 'wait-job.js', 'wait'), {callback: () => {
            console.log('submit Worker callback');
          }});
        },
        dependencies: ['default@PreBuild'],
        postDependencies: ['assembleHap'],
      });
    }
  }
}

export default {
  system: hapTasks /* Built-in plugin of Hvigor. It cannot be modified. */,
  plugins: [customPlugin()] /* Custom plugin to extend the functionality of Hvigor. */,  
};
```
 
 
wait-job.js内容如下，和hvigorfile.ts在同一个目录下：
 
```text
function sleep(ms) {
    return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
}

async function wait() {
    console.log('开始等待10秒...');
    await sleep(10000);
    console.log('结束，退出程序。');
}

exports.wait = wait;
```
 

##### WorkerOption

设置向线程池提交worker的配置，具体提交方式请参考[submitWorker](#section94763341419)。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 6.0.4
  
| 成员 | 声明 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| workInput | workInput?: unknown; | 设置要执行的线程的输入值。 |
| priority | priority?: Priority; | 设置线程执行的优先级。 |
| targetWorkers | targetWorkers?: number[]; | 指定要在几号线程中执行。 |
| callback | callback?: Function; | 执行完毕的回调函数。 |
| callbackInput | callbackInput?: unknown[]; | 回调函数的入参。 |
| useReturnVal | useReturnVal?: boolean; | 回调函数入参是否使用线程执行结束的返回值，优先级高于callbackInput。 |
 
 
 

##### Priority

线程执行的优先级枚举。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 6.0.4
  
| 成员 | 说明 |
| --- | --- |
| FIRST | 从上到下，优先级依次降低。 |
| HEAVY | 从上到下，优先级依次降低。 |
| MEDIUM | 从上到下，优先级依次降低。 |
| LIGHT | 从上到下，优先级依次降低。 |
| LAST | 从上到下，优先级依次降低。 |
 
 
 

##### TCB

向线程池提交worker后返回的状态，具体提交方式请参考[submitWorker](#section94763341419)。
 
**起始版本：**Hvigor 6.0.4
  
| 成员 | 声明 | 说明 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| getId | getId(): string; | 获取TCB自身的id。 |
| getWorkerId | getWorkerId(): number \| undefined; | 获取worker的id。 |
| getSubmitTime | getSubmitTime(): number; | 获取提交时间。 |
| getStartTime | getStartTime(): number \| undefined; | 获取执行开始时间。 |
| getEndTime | getEndTime(): number \| undefined; | 获取执行结束时间。 |
| getState | getState(): TaskState; | 获取worker状态。 |
| getPriority | getPriority(): Priority; | 获取优先级。 |
| getCallback | getCallback(): Function; | 获取回调函数。 |
| getCallbackInput | getCallbackInput(): unknown[]; | 获取回调函数的输入。 |
| getTaskPath | getTaskPath(): string; | 获取任务路径。 |
| getTaskName | getTaskName(): string; | 获取任务名。 |
| getTaskCompletePath | getTaskCompletePath(): string; | 获取任务完整路径，包含任务路径和任务名。 |
| useReturnVal | useReturnVal(): boolean; | 回调函数是否使用线程执行结束的返回值作为输入。 |
